## Findings Detail (Top Critical & High Risk)

### рџ”ґ CRITICAL (80/100)

**Location**: `/home/shogun/Documents/CDLab/implicit-conversion-hazard/OSS-Codebases/sqlite/ext/fts3/tool/fts3view.c:575:9`  
**Conversion**: `sqlite3_int64` в†’ `unsigned long long` (`IntegralCast`)

> CRITICAL (80/100): signed/unsigned comparison mismatch вЂ” classic bug pattern

```c
    if( iPrefix+nTerm+1 >= sizeof(zTerm) ){
        ^
```

**Fix**: Signed/unsigned comparison mismatch detected. Options:
  1. Cast the unsigned operand to signed if you know it is always non-negative: static_cast<sqlite3_int64>(unsigned_value)
  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned long long

```c
  for(i=0; i<(int)(sizeof(aFunc)/sizeof(aFunc[0])) && rc==SQLITE_OK; i++){
             ^
```

**Fix**: Signed/unsigned comparison mismatch detected. Options:
  1. Cast the unsigned operand to signed if you know it is always non-negative: static_cast<int>(unsigned_value)
  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned int

**Location**: `/home/shogun/Documents/CDLab/implicit-conversion-hazard/OSS-Codebases/sqlite/ext/misc/rot13.c:57:7`  
**Conversion**: `int` в†’ `unsigned long` (`IntegralCast`)

> CRITICAL (80/100): signed/unsigned comparison mismatch вЂ” classic bug pattern

```c
  if( nIn<sizeof(zTemp)-1 ){
      ^
```

**Fix**: Signed/unsigned comparison mismatch detected. Options:
  1. Cast the unsigned operand to signed if you know it is always non-negative: static_cast<int>(unsigned_value)
  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned long

### рџ”ґ CRITICAL (80/100)

**Location**: `/home/shogun/Documents/CDLab/implicit-conversion-hazard/OSS-Codebases/sqlite/ext/recover/test_recover.c:303:12`  
**Conversion**: `int` в†’ `unsigned long` (`IntegralCast`)

> CRITICAL (80/100): signed/unsigned comparison mismatch вЂ” classic bug pattern

```c
  for(i=0; i<sizeof(aCmd)/sizeof(struct Cmd); i++){
           ^
```

**Fix**: Signed/unsigned comparison mismatch detected. Options:
  1. Cast the unsigned operand to signed if you know it is always non-negative: static_cast<int>(unsigned_value)
  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned long

> CRITICAL (80/100): signed/unsigned comparison mismatch вЂ” classic bug pattern

```c
      if( op_none==op ) op = op_set;
          ^
```

**Fix**: Signed/unsigned comparison mismatch detected. Options:
  1. Cast the unsigned operand to signed if you know it is always non-negative: static_cast<int>(unsigned_value)
  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned int

```c
  for(i=0; i<sizeof(aObjCmd)/sizeof(aObjCmd[0]); i++){
           ^
```

**Fix**: Signed/unsigned comparison mismatch detected. Options:
  1. Cast the unsigned operand to signed if you know it is always non-negative: static_cast<int>(unsigned_value)
  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned long

---

ed long` (`IntegralCast`)

> CRITICAL (80/100): signed/unsigned comparison mismatch вЂ” classic bug pattern

```c
  for(ii=0; ii<sizeof(aCmd)/sizeof(aCmd[0]); ii++){
            ^
```

**Fix**: Signed/unsigned comparison mismatch detected. Options:
  1. Cast the unsigned operand to signed if you know it is always non-negative: static_cast<int>(unsigned_value)
  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned long

---

**Conversion**: `int` в†’ `unsigned long` (`IntegralCast`)

> CRITICAL (80/100): signed/unsigned comparison mismatch вЂ” classic bug pattern

```c

           ^
```

**Fix**: Signed/unsigned comparison mismatch detected. Options:
  1. Cast the unsigned operand to signed if you know it is always non-negative: static_cast<int>(unsigned_value)
  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned long

**Location**: `/home/shogun/Documents/CDLab/implicit-conversion-hazard/OSS-Codebases/sqlite/test/threadtest2.c:123:12`  
**Conversion**: `int` в†’ `unsigned long` (`IntegralCast`)

> CRITICAL (80/100): signed/unsigned comparison mismatch вЂ” classic bug pattern

```c
  for(i=0; i<sizeof(aThread)/sizeof(aThread[i]); i++){
           ^
```

**Fix**: Signed/unsigned comparison mismatch detected. Options:
  1. Cast the unsigned operand to signed if you know it is always non-negative: static_cast<int>(unsigned_value)
  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned long

  1. Cast the unsigned operand to signed if you know it is always non-negative: static_cast<int>(unsigned_value)
  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned long

  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned int

## Findings Detail (Top Critical & High Risk)

### рџ”ґ CRITICAL (80/100)

**Location**: `/home/shogun/Documents/CDLab/implicit-conversion-hazard/OSS-Codebases/sqlite/ext/misc/sqlar.c:89:16`  
**Conversion**: `sqlite3_int64` в†’ `unsigned long long` (`IntegralCast`)

> CRITICAL (80/100): signed/unsigned comparison mismatch вЂ” classic bug pattern

```c
  if( sz<=0 || sz==(nData = sqlite3_value_bytes(argv[0])) ){
               ^
```

**Fix**: Signed/unsigned comparison mismatch detected. Options:
  1. Cast the unsigned operand to signed if you know it is always non-negative: static_cast<sqlite3_int64>(unsigned_value)
  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned long long

### рџ”ґ CRITICAL (80/100)

**Location**: `/home/shogun/Documents/CDLab/implicit-conversion-hazard/OSS-Codebases/sqlite/ext/recover/test_recover.c:303:12`  
**Conversion**: `int` в†’ `unsigned long` (`IntegralCast`)

> CRITICAL (80/100): signed/unsigned comparison mismatch вЂ” classic bug pattern

```c
  for(i=0; i<sizeof(aCmd)/sizeof(struct Cmd); i++){
           ^
```

**Fix**: Signed/unsigned comparison mismatch detected. Options:
  1. Cast the unsigned operand to signed if you know it is always non-negative: static_cast<int>(unsigned_value)
  2. Change the signed variable to unsigned if it should never be negative
  3. Use a common wider signed type for both operands
  4. Add an assertion: assert(signed_value >= 0) before the comparison
  Other operand type: unsigned long
